% A_{\dot{b} \dot{a}}
% end_orig

\end{dmath*}

% -A_{\dot{a} \dot{b}}
% end_orig

\end{dmath*}

{\color[named]{Blue}\begin{verbatim}
RtoG:=R^{\lambda?}_{\mu?\nu?\kappa?} ->
-\partial_{\kappa?}{\Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu?\nu?}}
+\partial_{\nu?}{\Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu?\kappa?}}
-\Gamma^{\eta}_{\mu?\nu?} \Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\kappa?\eta}
+\Gamma^{\eta}_{\mu?\kappa?} \Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\nu?\eta};
\end{verbatim}}
% orig
% R^{\lambda?}_{\mu? \nu? \kappa?} -> ( - \partial_{\kappa?}{\Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu? \nu?}} + \partial_{\nu?}{\Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu? \kappa?}} - \Gamma^{\eta}_{\mu? \nu?} \Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\kappa? \eta} + \Gamma^{\eta}_{\mu? \kappa?} \Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\nu? \eta})
% end_orig
\begin{dmath*}[compact, spread=2pt]
RtoG\specialcolon{}= {R}^{\lambda?}\,_{\mu? \nu? \kappa?} \rightarrow ( - {\partial}_{\kappa?}{{\Gamma}^{\lambda?}\,_{\mu? \nu?}}\,  + {\partial}_{\nu?}{{\Gamma}^{\lambda?}\,_{\mu? \kappa?}}\,  - {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{\mu? \nu?} {\Gamma}^{\lambda?}\,_{\kappa? \eta} + {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{\mu? \kappa?} {\Gamma}^{\lambda?}\,_{\nu? \eta});
\end{dmath*}
{\color[named]{Blue}\begin{verbatim}
Gtog:=\Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu?\nu?} ->
(1/2)*g^{\lambda?\kappa} (
\partial_{\nu?}{g_{\kappa\mu?}} + \partial_{\mu?}{g_{\kappa\nu?}}-\partial_{\kappa}{g_{\mu?\nu?}});
\end{verbatim}}
% orig
% \Gamma^{\lambda?}_{\mu? \nu?} -> 1/2 g^{\lambda? \kappa} (\partial_{\nu?}{g_{\kappa \mu?}} + \partial_{\mu?}{g_{\kappa \nu?}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{\mu? \nu?}})
% end_orig
\begin{dmath*}[compact, spread=2pt]

\end{dmath*}

{\color[named]{Blue}\begin{verbatim}

@distribute!(%);@prodrule!(%);@distribute!(%);@prodsort!(%);
\end{verbatim}}
% orig
% ( - \partial_{4}{\Gamma^{m1}_{4 n}} + \partial_{n}{\Gamma^{m1}_{4 4}} - \Gamma^{\eta}_{4 n} \Gamma^{m1}_{4 \eta} + \Gamma^{\eta}_{4 4} \Gamma^{m1}_{n \eta}) g_{m1 m} + ( - \partial_{4}{\Gamma^{4}_{4 n}} + \partial_{n}{\Gamma^{4}_{4 4}} - \Gamma^{\eta}_{4 n} \Gamma^{4}_{4 \eta} + \Gamma^{\eta}_{4 4} \Gamma^{4}_{n \eta}) g_{4 m}
% end_orig
\begin{dmath*}[compact, spread=2pt]
todo\specialcolon{}= ( - {\partial}_{4}{{\Gamma}^{m1}\,_{4 n}}\,  + {\partial}_{n}{{\Gamma}^{m1}\,_{4 4}}\,  - {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{4 n} {\Gamma}^{m1}\,_{4 \eta} + {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{4 4} {\Gamma}^{m1}\,_{n \eta}) {g}_{m1 m} + ( - {\partial}_{4}{{\Gamma}^{4}\,_{4 n}}\,  + {\partial}_{n}{{\Gamma}^{4}\,_{4 4}}\,  - {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{4 n} {\Gamma}^{4}\,_{4 \eta} + {\Gamma}^{\eta}\,_{4 4} {\Gamma}^{4}\,_{n \eta}) {g}_{4 m};
\end{dmath*}
% orig
% ( - \partial_{4}{(1/2 g^{m1 \kappa} (\partial_{n}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa n}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 n}}))} + \partial_{n}{(1/2 g^{m1 \kappa} (\partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 4}}))} - 1/4 g^{\eta \kappa} (\partial_{n}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa n}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 n}}) g^{m1 \mu} (\partial_{\eta}{g_{\mu 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\mu \eta}} - \partial_{\mu}{g_{4 \eta}}) + 1/4 g^{\eta \kappa} (\partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 4}}) g^{m1 \mu} (\partial_{\eta}{g_{\mu n}} + \partial_{n}{g_{\mu \eta}} - \partial_{\mu}{g_{n \eta}})) g_{m1 m} + ( - \partial_{4}{(1/2 g^{4 \kappa} (\partial_{n}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa n}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 n}}))} + \partial_{n}{(1/2 g^{4 \kappa} (\partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 4}}))} - 1/4 g^{\eta \kappa} (\partial_{n}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa n}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 n}}) g^{4 \mu} (\partial_{\eta}{g_{\mu 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\mu \eta}} - \partial_{\mu}{g_{4 \eta}}) + 1/4 g^{\eta \kappa} (\partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} + \partial_{4}{g_{\kappa 4}} - \partial_{\kappa}{g_{4 4}}) g^{4 \mu} (\partial_{\eta}{g_{\mu n}} + \partial_{n}{g_{\mu \eta}} - \partial_{\mu}{g_{n \eta}})) g_{4 m}

{\color[named]{Blue}\begin{verbatim}
@substitute!(%)(g_{4 4} ->\phi): @substitute!(%){g_{4 m} ->\phi A_{m});
@substitute!(%)(g_{m n} -> \phi**{-1} h_{m n}+\phi A_{m} A_{n});
@substitute!(%)(g^{4 4}) -> \phi**{-1}+\phi a_{m} h^{m n} A_{n}):
